# Task 1
only task 1 using the Agility pack has been done. the better approach is that we using the AI based on ML and Onnx.
it needs some exceptions to be thrown manually in case of invalid html and for a patern which is null or invlid.
also the whole parsing class can be dynamic by storing the properties and apperns into DB.
this gives a better versioning too.
needs more unit tests.

## Run
docker-compose -f docker-compose.yml up




## Grpc
for grpc checking, you can use below command. fix proto **include folder** as your clones directory.
`grpcui -proto dataExtractor.proto -import-path "C:\projects\Test\fynd\API\02.Services\FyndParser\Fynd.Parser.Endpoint\Grpc\Proto" -plaintext localhost:5000`
we can add grpc reflectin too.

## Rest
post below json content to http://localhost:5001/api/DataExtractor/Extract. according integration tests.

data-coords=\",\" rel=\"\" id=\"with-city-centre-polygon\">\r\nShow map\r\n<\/a>\r\n<\/span>\r\n<\/h3>\r\n<\/div>\r\n<p>This 5-star hotel on Berlin\u2019s Kurf\u00FCrstendamm shopping street offers elegant rooms, an indoor pool and great public transport links. It is 600 metres from the Ged\u00E4chtniskirche Church and Berlin Zoo.<\/p>\r\n<p>Kempinski Hotel Bristol Berlin offers air-conditioned rooms with large windows, modern bathrooms and international TV channels. Bathrobes are provided. Free WiFi is available in all areas and high-speed WiFi access can be booked at an additional cost.<\/p>\r\n<p>Gourmet cuisine is served in the popular Kempinski Grill. Reinhard's brasserie offer light cuisine and a terrace overlooking Kurf\u00FCrstendamm. Guests can enjoy drinks in the Gobelin Halle lounge or in the Bristol Bar.<\/p>\r\n<p>Kempinski Bristol Berlin\u2019s spa includes a sauna, steam room and gym. Massages and beauty treatments can also be booked here. The hotel's business centre can be used free of charge.<\/p>\r\n<p>Uhlandstra\u00DFe Underground Station is just outside the Kempinski\u2019s front door. The KaDeWe shopping mall is 2 stops away. \r\n<br><\/p>\r\n<\/div>\r\n<div data-component=\"track\" data-track=\"view\" data-hash=\"HMDOTECfSeUdWMMKXe\" data-stage=\"1\"><\/div>\r\n<p class=\"revd_policy revd_collapsible lock_price v2 clearfix  policy_margin_fix\">\r\n<div id=\"rev_policy_left\">\r\n<i class=\"policy_icon\">\uB231<\/i>\r\n<\/div>\r\n<div id=\"rev_policy_right\">\r\n<h3 class=\"verified_reviews\">100% verified reviews<\/h3>\r\n<p class=\"policy_subs\">Real guests. Real stays. Real opinions.<\/p>\r\n<\/div>\r\n<div class=\"policy_more\">\r\n<a href=\"http:\/\/www.booking.com\/hotel\/de\/kempinskibristolberlin.en-gb.html?label=gen173nr-15CAsoO0IWa2VtcGluc2tpYnJpc3RvbGJlcmxpbkguYgVub3JlZmg7iAEBmAEuuAEEyAEE2AED6AEB;sid=76794d5ed9a9673c09a746b2d3e1a5bd;dcid=4;dist=0&sb_price_type=total&type=total&#\" id=\"guidelines_open_link\" class=\"no_underline v_review_modal js-guidelines_open_link\">Read more<\/a>\r\n<\/div>\r\n<\/div>\r\n<style>\r\n.guidelines_content {\r\nbackground: #fff;\r\npadding: 12px 24px;\r\ntext-align: justify;\r\ncolor: #003580;\r\n}\r\n.guidelines_content_lightbox {\r\nbackground: #fff;\r\npadding: 12px 24px;\r\ntext-align: justify;\r\nheight: 400px;\r\noverflow-y: scroll;\r\ncolor: #003580;\r\n}\r\n.guidelines_content p,\r\n.guidelines_content_lightbox p {\r\nmargin: 1em 0;\r\n}\r\n.guidelines_content .head,\r\n.guidelines_content_lightbox .head {\r\nfont-weight: bold;\r\nfont-size: 16px;\r\n}\r\n@media (max-device-width: 600px) {\r\n.guidelines_content {\r\nwidth: auto;\r\ntext-align: left;\r\n}\r\n}\r\n<\/style>\r\n<div id=\"guidelines_content\" class=\"guidelines_content_lightbox\" style=\"display:none;\">\r\n<p class=\"headline\">Booking.com guest review guidelines<\/p>\r\n<i>To keep the rating score and review content relevant for your upcoming trip, we archive reviews older than 24 months.<\/i>\r\n<p>Only a customer who has booked through Booking.com and stayed at the property in question can write a review. This lets us know that our reviews come from real guests, like you. Who better to tell others about the free breakfast, friendly staff, or quiet room than someone who\u2019s stayed at the property before?<\/p>\r\n<p>We want you to share your story, both the good and the bad. All we ask is that you follow a few simple guidelines.<\/p>\r\n<p class=\"head\">Tips for writing a great review<\/p>\r\n<p><strong>Give us details.<\/strong> People love to hear about the details. Was the air-conditioning working? Was there a chocolate on your pillow? We like long reviews and suggest you write at least 50 words.<\/p>\r\n<p><strong>Be candid.<\/strong> Give us your honest opinion. We\u2019ll never remove a review just because it\u2019s negative. That's our promise to you.<\/p>\r\n<p><strong>Be relevant.<\/strong> The best reviews provide constructive information that helps other travellers to make better choices. Stay on topic and avoid content that others might find offensive.<\/p>\r\n<p class=\"head\">We will sometimes remove reviews if they include the following:<\/p>\r\n<p><strong>Objectionable material.<\/strong> This includes insulting or discriminatory remarks, swearing or offensive language.<\/p>\r\n<p><strong>Private information.<\/strong> To protect your privacy (and that of others) we do not display reviews that include email addresses or phone numbers.<\/p>\r\n<p><strong>Sensitive information.<\/strong> We do not display reviews that contain information with possible legal implications. This includes references to suspected illegal conduct or allusions to lost or stolen items. In such sensitive cases, you should contact Customer Service, who will be happy to help.<\/p>\r\n<p><strong>Irrelevant topics.<\/strong> This includes promotional content and politically sensitive subjects.<\/p>\r\n<p class=\"head\">In some rare cases, neither the written review nor the review score can be displayed. This only happens when:<\/p>\r\n<p><strong>Key information is missing.<\/strong> A few review questions are mandatory. If these aren\u2019t answered, we aren't able to calculate a fair review score, so we can't display the review.<\/p>\r\n<p><strong>You didn\u2019t stay at the property.<\/strong> When necessary, we\u2019ll confirm this information with both you and the accommodation owner.<\/p>\r\n<p><strong>You made a mistake.<\/strong> Everyone makes mistakes. We won\u2019t post yours. If you reviewed a different property from the one you booked, let us know. We can fix it so that your review goes with the right property.<\/p>\r\n<p><strong>The review is a fake.<\/strong> If there is any indication that a review is not authentic or is in any way fraudulent it will be flagged during the moderation process.<\/p>\r\n<\/div>\r\n<div id=\"review_list_score\" class=\"review_list_score_container lang_ltr\">\r\n<div
